Exploring Network Management Challenges and the Benefits of Outsourcing

Virtually every business needs to do more with less, and IT is no exception. At the same time, the network has to meet the growing demands of the business. New research conducted by IDG explores the network management challenges that IT and telecom leaders face and how they are dealing with them. A majority said they would consider outsourcing network management. Would you? Learn more about the research results.

Eliminating the Challenge of Branch Office Recovery

Backup and replication practices in remote offices can be erratic and error prone. Discover how a branch converged infrastructure brings this critical function into the data center enabling organizations to:
- Meet the resiliency needs of remote locales
- Restore branch operations is minutes vs. days
- Avoid risks of downtime and data loss in remote locations
- Take the burden off the edge while ensuring applications still feel local to end users
